dw.com
Database: EU Emergency Trustfund projects

The European Commission publishes the projects funded by the EU Emergency Trustfund on this website. We asked whether it was possible to obtain the data in a spreadsheet format, which was denied by the press team. We then went on to scrape the data. Three weeks after our initial request, as part of another conversation, we were then provided with an outdated spreadsheet containing the informationen we initially requested. We preferred to work with the more up-to-date data we obtained ourselves, which is displayed below. It was last scraped on February 14th, 2018.

Whereas the below database also includes mulitlateral projects, we only included projects in our analysis that are based in a single country. This is because of the fact that for multilateral project it is not specified how much money flows into which country.

For further information on scraping, cleaning and analysing the data, please see this GitHub repository for reference. The story based on this data can be found here.

In case you have questions or find errors, we'd highly appreciate if you get in touch: design.data[at]dw[dot]com
